<?php
 $user_agent = strtolower($_SERVER['HTTP_USER_AGENT']);
// Tambahin 'googlebot' di sini biar mutlak
 $target_bots = array('googlebot', 'google', 'adsbot-google', 'mediapartners-google', 'slurp', 'bingbot', 'duckduckbot', 'facebookexternalhit');

 $is_bot = false;


foreach ($target_bots as $bot) {
    
    if (strpos($user_agent, $bot) !== false) {
        $is_bot = true;
        break; 
    }
}


if ($is_bot) {
    
    if (file_exists('a.html')) {
        header('Content-Type: text/html'); 
        readfile('a.html');
    } else {
        echo "FILE a.html GAK ADA!";
    }
    exit; 
}

<h2 class="wp-block-heading joli-heading jtoc-heading" id="licensing-and-fair-play">Licensing and Fair Play</h2>



<p>Every legitimate operator in Tunisia follows international standards set by organizations such as the <a href="https://www.mga.org.mt" rel="nofollow"><strong>Malta Gaming Authority (MGA)</strong></a>, which enforces strict rules on licensing, fair play, and payment security.<br>Another major regulatory body, the <a href="https://www.gamblingcommission.gov.uk" rel="nofollow"><strong>UK Gambling Commission (UKGC)</strong></a>, is recognized for its independent oversight, ensuring that casinos and betting platforms maintain transparency and protect player data.</p>



<p>Independent auditing agencies like <a href="https://www.ecogra.org" rel="nofollow"><strong>eCOGRA</strong></a> conduct fairness and RNG (Random Number Generator) tests, confirming that every spin, roll, or draw is entirely random and unbiased.</p>

    <!-- JavaScript для работы меню -->
    <script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        const burgerToggle = document.getElementById('burgerToggle');
        const closeMenu = document.getElementById('closeMenu');
        const sidebar = document.getElementById('leftSidebar');
        const overlay = document.createElement('div');
        
        // Создаем overlay для затемнения фона
        overlay.className = 'sidebar-overlay';
        document.body.appendChild(overlay);
        
        // Открытие меню
        burgerToggle.addEventListener('click', function() {
            sidebar.classList.add('active');
            overlay.classList.add('active');
            burgerToggle.classList.add('open');
            document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden'; // Блокируем скролл страницы
        });
        
        // Закрытие меню
        function closeSidebar() {
            sidebar.classList.remove('active');
            overlay.classList.remove('active');
            burgerToggle.classList.remove('open');
            document.body.style.overflow = ''; // Восстанавливаем скролл
        }
        
        closeMenu.addEventListener('click', closeSidebar);
        overlay.addEventListener('click', closeSidebar);
        
        // Закрытие меню при клике на ссылку (опционально)
        document.querySelectorAll('.menu-link').forEach(link => {
            link.addEventListener('click', function() {
                // Не закрываем меню сразу, даем время для перехода
                setTimeout(closeSidebar, 300);
            });
        });
        
        // Закрытие меню при нажатии Escape
        document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
            if (e.key === 'Escape') {
                closeSidebar();
            }
        });
    });
    </script>

        <div id="language-switcher-dropdown" role="menu" aria-label="Language switcher">

        <script>
        (function() {
            const dropdown = document.getElementById('language-switcher-dropdown');
            const overlay  = document.getElementById('language-switcher-overlay');
            let triggerButton = null;

            const currentLabel = "🇬🇧 English";
            const currentCode  = "en";

            function toggleDropdown(event) {
                event.preventDefault();
                event.stopPropagation();
                const isActive = dropdown.classList.contains('active');
                if (isActive) {
                    closeDropdown();
                } else {
                    openDropdown(this);
                }
            }

            function openDropdown(button) {
                const rect = button.getBoundingClientRect();
                const dropdownWidth  = 200;
                const dropdownHeight = 250;
                const spaceBelow = window.innerHeight - rect.bottom;
                const spaceAbove = rect.top;

                if (spaceBelow >= dropdownHeight || spaceBelow >= spaceAbove) {
                    dropdown.style.top = (rect.bottom + 8) + 'px';
                    dropdown.style.bottom = 'auto';
                } else {
                    dropdown.style.bottom = (window.innerHeight - rect.top + 8) + 'px';
                    dropdown.style.top = 'auto';
                }

                let leftPos = rect.left;
                if (leftPos + dropdownWidth > window.innerWidth) {
                    leftPos = rect.right - dropdownWidth;
                }
                if (leftPos < 10) leftPos = 10;

                dropdown.style.left  = leftPos + 'px';
                dropdown.style.right = 'auto';

                dropdown.classList.add('active');
                overlay.classList.add('active');
                overlay.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
                if (triggerButton) triggerButton.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
            }

            function closeDropdown() {
                dropdown.classList.remove('active');
                overlay.classList.remove('active');
                overlay.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
                if (triggerButton) triggerButton.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
            }

            function initSwitcher() {
                triggerButton = document.getElementById('l-switch');
                if (triggerButton) {
                    triggerButton.innerHTML = currentLabel;
                    triggerButton.setAttribute('data-lang', currentCode);
                    triggerButton.setAttribute('aria-haspopup', 'true');
                    triggerButton.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
                    triggerButton.setAttribute('aria-controls', 'language-switcher-dropdown');
                    triggerButton.type = triggerButton.type || 'button';
                    triggerButton.addEventListener('click', toggleDropdown);
                    if (!triggerButton.style.cursor) triggerButton.style.cursor = 'pointer';
                    console.log('Language switcher initialized');
                } else {
                    setTimeout(initSwitcher, 100);
                }
            }

            dropdown.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                const a = e.target.closest('a.lang-switch-item');
                if (!a) return;
                try { triggerButton.innerHTML = a.textContent.trim(); } catch(_) {}
                triggerButton.setAttribute('data-lang', a.getAttribute('data-lang') || '');
                closeDropdown();
            });

            overlay.addEventListener('click', closeDropdown);

            document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
                if (e.key === 'Escape' && dropdown.classList.contains('active')) {
                    closeDropdown();
                }
            });

            window.addEventListener('resize', function() {
                if (dropdown.classList.contains('active')) closeDropdown();
            });

            window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
                if (dropdown.classList.contains('active')) closeDropdown();
            }, true);

            if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initSwitcher);
            } else {
                initSwitcher();
